< Review>
We take part in the Passport 2 History (look it up if you don't know about it) and three of the passport museums are within walking distance of each other in Santa Paula!  So my son and I took a day trip out to Santa Paula.  We visited all three museums starting with The California Oil Museum!

This FREE museum has a lot of stuff and has an excellent presentation!  What I liked best was that there are a ton of things for little kids to do... push buttons and stuff happens and what not.  There is a lot of cool antique gasolina here, signs, bulbs, etc.

You won't spend too-too much time here, but make this your first stop, park in the lot and make your way to the other museums as well.  A great day trip!<//Review>

< text>
This is a simple, clean, attentive place. The staff is nice and the menu has a variety with more than one vegetarian option. It's 3.50 for one empanada, but there are combo and bulk options. The size of each is not that large, the meal of 3 could fill you, but if you are really hungry than maybe not.

I tried the veggie, corn, and mushroom ones. My favorite was the corn, it had the most flavor, but then all of them did had flavor and tasted good. The only thing is that they seemed a little burnt, but nothing too bad. Still a good option for a food that's not widely available in SD.<//text>

<pics>None< /pics><Time>1526091349467</Time><Review>Very good potential. Maybe this place is best at lunch. Went at about 6:30pm and they had most empanadas still available. That was good. Got the ratatouille, daily special Italian sausage, ham n cheese, goat cheese and mushroom, and chicken. Ingredients inside were very flavorful and hit the spot. I was pleased with the portion size and value.

I would have preferred a crispier crust on most of the empanadas. They sit in a heated cabinet waiting to be pulled for orders. I think they could easily add a quick air fryer prior to serving, to heat up the filling a bit more and also that would crisp up the exterior a bit. That would elevate this place a bunch.

Also the chimichurri side is a bit lacking. It's too vinegary and watery. Totally not a dipping sauce and basically not what most would think of as a chimichurri sauce. Not green. If they offered maybe a few dipping options, I could see that being a big plus to complement various flavors of empanadas.</Review><userid>114450886917289319592</userid>< Rating>
